### [1] [Gaussian Reformulation of the Feynman Path Integral for Quantum Statistical Mechanics with Results for the Second Virial Coefficient of $^4$He](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16301)
*Phil Attard*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于高斯采样的费曼路径积分新方法，用于量子统计力学计算，避免了传统路径积分蒙特卡洛中多温度节点和数值抵消的问题，并通过氦气第二维里系数的理论与实验对比验证了方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统路径积分量子蒙特卡洛方法在处理量子统计力学问题时，需要对每个构型设置多个温度节点，并在统计平均中进行数值抵消，这带来了计算复杂性和数值不稳定性的问题。因此，需要一种更高效、数值更稳定的新算法。

Method: 将费曼路径积分重新表述为对每个位置构型邻域的高斯采样。方差通过晶格上的环聚合物统计获得，均值通过Wigner-Kirkwood对易函数的高温展开得到。该方法避免了传统方法中每个构型需要多个温度节点以及统计平均中的数值抵消问题。

Result: 通过氦气第二维里系数的解析计算和模拟结果，与实验室测量数据进行了对比验证。

Conclusion: 提出的高斯采样路径积分方法有效克服了传统路径积分量子蒙特卡洛的数值困难，为量子统计力学计算提供了新的途径，且与实验数据吻合良好。

Abstract: The Feynman path integral for quantum statistical mechanics is reformulated as Gaussian sampling of the neighborhood of each position configuration. The variance and mean are obtained from ring polymer statistics on a lattice, and from the high temperature expansion of the Wigner-Kirkwood commutation function, respectively. The algorithm avoids multiple temperature nodes for each configuration and the need for numerical cancelation in the statistical averages, which are problematic for conventional path integral quantum Monte Carlo. Analytic and simulation results for the second virial coefficient of helium are compared to laboratory measurements.

</details>


### [2] [Representation-Dependent Machine Learning of the Isotropic-Nematic Transition in the Lebwohl-Lasher Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16481)
*Maninder Kaur,Aojie Xue,David P Landau*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了无监督机器学习在检测Lebwohl-Lasher模型各向同性-向列相变时，输入表示是否保持系统对称性的关键作用。原始分子构型因旋转简并性导致PCA和卷积自编码器失败，而旋转不变的局域关联表示则能成功检测相变；有监督3D CNN则能从原始构型预测序参量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究机器学习检测相变时，输入表示是否保持系统对称性对检测效果的影响，特别是在具有连续简并性的取向有序系统中。

Method: 使用无监督学习（PCA、卷积自编码器CAE）和有监督学习（3D CNN）分别处理Lebwohl-Lasher模型的原始构型和旋转不变的局域关联表示，对比检测相变的效果。

Result: 无监督方法（PCA、CAE）在原始构型上无法检测相变，但在旋转不变表示上能恢复相变信号和双峰共存分布；有监督3D CNN在给定标签条件下能从原始构型准确预测标量序参量。

Conclusion: Lebwohl-Lasher模型分离了无监督相发现与有监督序参量回归，表明在取向有序系统中，无监督机器学习需要对称性保持的输入表示。

Abstract: Machine-learning detection of phase transitions depends not only on the learning algorithm, but also on whether the input representation preserves the symmetries of the system. We examine this for the weak first-order isotropic--nematic transition of the three-dimensional Lebwohl--Lasher model, whose apolar and continuously degenerate nematic phase makes raw molecular configurations a challenging input for unsupervised learning. Principal component analysis (PCA) and a convolutional autoencoder (CAE) fail to identify the transition from raw configurations because rotationally equivalent nematic states can appear far apart in the input space. When the same configurations are transformed into a rotationally invariant local-correlation representation, both methods recover transition-sensitive signatures and bimodal coexistence distributions. A supervised three-dimensional convolutional neural network (CNN), by contrast, accurately predicts the scalar order parameter from raw configurations when given order-parameter labels. The Lebwohl-Lasher model therefore separates unsupervised phase discovery from supervised order-parameter regression and shows that symmetry-respecting input representations are needed for unsupervised machine learning in orientationally ordered systems.

</details>


### [3] [Glauber dynamics phase transitions in athermal random field Blume-Capel and Blume-Emery-Grifitths models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16561)
*Sumedha,Aldrin B E*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了完全图上 Glauber 动力学与平衡态下随机场 Ising 模型和 Blume-Emery-Griffiths 模型的稳态行为，发现高斯随机场方差 R 类似于温度，存在临界值 R_c；当 R 低于 R_c 时稳态依赖初始态，高于 R_c 时动力学稳态与平衡态一致；同时分析了磁滞回线的形状、矫顽场以及丰富的相图行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究 Glauber 动力学在随机场模型中的非平衡稳态与平衡态之间的关系，揭示方差 R 作为类温度参数的作用，以及引入排斥双二次相互作用后模型的临界行为变化。

Method: 在完全图上解析求解 Glauber 动力学的稳态，并与平衡态结果进行比较；通过分析高斯随机场方差 R 的临界值 R_c 刻画相变；考虑 Blume-Emery-Griffiths 模型中的排斥双二次相互作用和晶体场，研究磁滞回线形状与矫顽场。

Result: 发现 R 低于临界值 R_c 时，动力学稳态依赖于初始态；R 超过 R_c 时动力学稳态与平衡态一致；排斥双二次相互作用可使 R_c 降至零；系统可在演化中发生从 R_c=0 到 R_c=√(2/π) 的交叉行为；外场下存在矩形、六边形、平行四边形、蜂腰形和双磁滞回线等多种磁滞回线形状，其面积依赖 R 而形状由 R=0 决定。

Conclusion: 随机场方差 R 在 Glauber 动力学中扮演类似温度的角色，控制着非平衡稳态与平衡态的一致性；排斥双二次相互作用可显著改变临界行为；磁滞回线的解析表达式揭示了模型丰富的相图结构，且显著依赖于初始状态。

Abstract: We solve the two models for Glauber dynamics and in equilibrium, both in the presence and absence of the external magnetic field on a complete graph. We compare the steady state of the Glauber dynamics with equilibrium and find that for low values of variance $R$ of the Gaussian random field, the steady state of the Glauber dynamics depends on the initial state. Beyond a critical value $R_{c}$ the equilibrium and non equilibrium steady states coincide. The variance $R$ in random field models behaves similar to the temperature. The location of both the continuous and first order transitions can be obtained exactly for the Glauber dynamics steady state. The frustration is introduced by considering repulsive bi-quadratic interaction for Blume-Emery-Griffiths model. We also. consider repulsive bi-quadratic interaction and show that $R_c$ can become zero depending on the value of the crystal field. Interestingly, we also find that even when a system has $R_c=0$ at the start of quasi-static evolution with Glauber dynamics, with increasing $R$, in some regime of the couplings, the model undergoes a crossover to a random field Ising model universaility with $R_c$ changing from $0$ to $\sqrt{\frac{2}π}$. In the presence of uniform magnetic field, regions of first order transition exhibit hysteresis under Glauber dynamics. These models exhibit rectangular, hexagonal, parallelogram, wasp-waisted, and double hysteresis loops. We derive the shapes of hysteresis loops analytically giving the equation for the value of the coercive field and show that while the area under the hysteresis loop depends on $R$, the shape is determined by the behavior of the models at $R=0$. In particular, in the case of Blume-Emery-Griffiths model the hysteresis plots have regions of continuous and first order transitions both, resulting in a rich phase diagram that depends non-trivially on the initial state.

</details>


### [4] [On the Information Required for Feedback Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16639)
*Matthew P. Leighton,Jose M. Betancourt,Thierry Emonet,Benjamin B. Machta,Michael C. Abbott*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文研究了信息受限条件下随机系统的反馈控制问题，推导了控制器所需信息率的下界，并提出了一个最优控制协议——通过概率性地时间逆转被动动力学来饱和该下界。研究展示了该方法在非线性粒子定位、微生物导航和信息引擎等领域的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物系统以及许多工程问题需要在有限信息条件下控制噪声系统，而现有理论对信息受限控制的理论极限和最优策略尚不清晰。

Method: 采用信息论与随机控制相结合的方法，推导了从受控系统到控制器的信息率下界，并针对状态无关被动动力学的系统，提出了一个概率性时间逆转被动动力学的最优控制协议。

Result: 得到了信息受限控制问题的性能-信息帕累托前沿，并证明了所提出的时间反转协议可以饱和信息率下界。

Conclusion: 该框架为广泛的信息受限控制问题提供了理论极限和最优策略，并在粒子定位、微生物导航和信息引擎等应用中得到了验证。

Abstract: Biological systems across scales, along with many engineering problems, must control noisy systems with limited information. Here we study information-limited feedback control of stochastic systems to achieve target steady states, and derive a lower bound on the information rate from controlled system to controller. This framework allows us to obtain performance-information Pareto frontiers for wide-ranging control problems with limited information. For systems with state-independent passive dynamics, the bound is saturated by an explicit optimal control protocol which probabilistically time-reverses the passive dynamics. We showcase these results through applications to nonlinear particle localization, microbial navigation, and experimentally realized information engines.

</details>


### [5] [Occupation-condensation transition of a sublinearly vertex-reinforced random walk on regular tree](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16971)
*Bon A Koo,Edward Ju*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究b-ary树上的顶点强化随机游走(VRRW)，发现当记忆强度参数a∈(0,1)时，占据测度在临界值β_c(a,b)处发生尖锐凝聚相变：低于β_c时占据扩散且范围线性增长；高于β_c时单个顶点占据O(1)分数的时间，但范围仍缓慢增长（约log t速率），与有限区域局域化不同。通过四个估计量定位相同阈值，验证了可逆性、分枝数判据和共存现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解强记忆性（幂律强化）下随机游走在大规模树状结构上的占据行为，特别是凝聚相变及其与有限区域局域化的区别。

Method: 理论分析结合大规模数值模拟（t=3×10^7），使用四种估计量定位相变阈值；通过可逆性将问题转化为边电导模型和分支数判据；对不同分支数b=2,3,4进行bootstrap标度分析。

Result: 发现了尖锐的凝聚相变，临界阈值β_c与b-1成正比；凝聚态占据测度非自平均且双峰分布，呈现共存现象；低于阈值时范围线性增长，高于阈值时范围约log t增长。

Conclusion: VRRW在树上的凝聚相变是一种不同于有限区域局域化的新现象，其标度行为可由可逆性和分支数判据预测，为理解强记忆随机游走的临界行为提供了完整框架。

Abstract: A vertex-reinforced random walk steps to a neighbour with probability proportional to $1+βn^{a}$, where $n$ counts previous visits to that neighbour and $a\in(0,1)$ sets the memory strength. On the rooted $b$-ary tree the exponential growth of the vertex set drives the walk outward while the reinforcement pulls it back. We report a sharp condensation transition of the occupation measure at a finite $β_c(a,b)$: below it the occupation spreads and the range grows linearly; above it a single vertex holds an $O(1)$ fraction of the time, stable in the observation time, while the range keeps growing very slowly, at a rate better described by $\log t$ than by any power. We do not find the range to be bounded, and keep this condensation distinct from finite-range localization. Four estimators locate the same threshold, which shows no systematic drift out to $t=3\times10^{7}$. In a frozen environment the walk is reversible, with edge conductances $c_{uv}=w_{u}w_{v}$, $w_{v}=1+βn_{v}^{a}$, and measure $μ_{v}\propto w_{v}\sum_{u\sim v}w_{u}$ describing the condensed core, whose neighbour coupling we test directly. Reversibility places the escape at the frontier within the branching-number criterion for biased walks on trees, predicting $β_c\propto b-1$; the measured lines for $b=2,3,4$ collapse under division by $b-1$ to a few percent (bootstrap). The value $a=1/2$ that governs the walk on $\mathbb{Z}$ enters only as the marginal exponent of the condensed profile. Near $β_c$ the occupancy is non-self-averaging and bimodal, a coexistence-type phenomenology.

</details>


### [6] [Floquet Driving of Enzymatic Reactions: Counting Statistics and Long-Time Currents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17072)
*Yuki Watanabe,Yuki Ishiguro,Takashi Oka*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文发展了适用于经典随机过程的Floquet理论，用于计算周期性调制下化学反应的电流及其计数统计，并通过对离散驱动Michaelis-Menten模型的解析和数值分析，展示了周期切换反应速率如何产生长期产物电流，揭示了高频率极限下周期驱动可等效为化学反应速率修正的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着光遗传学等人工控制化学反应系统技术的快速发展，理解时间依赖控制下的反应动力学日益重要。当反应速率的调制在时间上具有周期性时，需要系统的理论框架来分析其动力学行为。

Method: 基于Floquet形式论，针对经典随机过程引入计数场，推导了第一次累积量及对应电流的通用表达式。电流通过有效Floquet生成元和“kick态”表示，并分别得到高、低频极限下的渐近表达式。以离散Floquet驱动（非微扰、阶跃式协议）为具体案例，将其应用于受G蛋白调控的cAMP生化反应系统，建立了离散驱动的Michaelis-Menten反应模型。

Result: 获得了周期切换反应速率下长期产物电流的解析表达式和数值结果。在高频极限下，周期性驱动的效应可等价于对化学反应速率的有效修正。

Conclusion: 本文为周期驱动化学反应系统的Floquet分析提供了理论基础，拓展了Floquet形式论在经典随机过程中的应用。

Abstract: Technologies for artificially controlling chemical reaction systems, such as optogenetics, are rapidly advancing, making it increasingly important to understand reaction dynamics under time-dependent control. When the modulation of reaction rates is periodic in time, the Floquet formalism provides a systematic framework. We develop a Floquet theory for classical stochastic processes that enables the calculation of the current and its counting statistics under such periodic modulation. In particular, we formulate the theory in terms of a counting field and derive general expressions for the first cumulant and the corresponding current. The current is expressed using the effective Floquet generator and the kicked state, and we further obtain general asymptotic expressions for the current in both the high- and low-frequency regimes. As a concrete example to test our analytical expressions, we then apply the results to discrete Floquet driving -- a non-perturbative, stepwise protocol. The setup is motivated by a biochemical system known as cyclic adenosine monophosphate (cAMP) production, which is an enzymatic reaction activated and inhibited by G-proteins. This is formulated as a discretely driven Michaelis--Menten-type reaction model, in which the catalytic activity is switched on and off abruptly in time, and we obtain analytical expressions and numerical results showing how periodic switching of reaction rates generates a long-time product current. In particular, in the high-frequency limit, we show that the effect of the periodic driving can be interpreted through an effective modification of the chemical reaction rates. These results provide a basis for Floquet analysis of periodically driven chemical reactions.

</details>


### [7] [Adverse Selection with Quality Variance: A Maximum-Entropy Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17239)
*Zhi-Lei Zhang,Tan-Ji Zhou,C. P. Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过将逆向选择建模为质量分布的动态截断过程，揭示了市场退化速度与质量分布演化的内在机制。研究发现：存在防止完全逆向选择的机制；质量方差越大或价格溢价越小，平均质量退化上限越高；最大熵基准分析表明质量方差与支付率共同决定市场退化及最终稳定质量平台。此外，提高买方支付率、降低质量方差或提高最低质量底线均可减缓逆向选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统逆向选择模型仅用平均质量描述市场，无法解释市场退化的速度及质量分布的动态演化过程，本文旨在解决这两个问题。

Method: 将逆向选择建模为质量分布的动态截断过程：买方设定一个高于平均质量的比例上限（参数ξ>1），超过该上限的卖方拒绝报价并退出市场，剩余市场由截断后的条件分布刻画，迭代该过程直至市场质量达到稳定状态。

Result: （i）识别出防止完全逆向选择的机制；（ii）质量方差越大或价格溢价越小，平均质量退化上限越高；（iii）通过最大熵基准数值分析，揭示了质量方差与支付率共同决定市场退化程度及最终稳定质量平台。

Conclusion: 提高买方支付率、降低质量方差或提高最低质量底线均可有效减缓逆向选择，为市场干预提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The adverse-selection mechanism in markets explains how asymmetric information between buyers and sellers can drive high-quality goods out of the market, thereby causing market deterioration. In its simplest formulation, only the mean quality is used to describe the market, and this is insufficient to determine how fast the market deteriorates or how the quality distribution evolves. To resolve the two problems, we describe the adverse selection as a dynamic truncation of the quality distribution: buyers set an upper bound proportional to the mean quality by a rate $ξ$ that is larger than unity, and sellers whose quality exceeds this upper bound reject an offer and exit the market. The retained market is then characterized by the conditional distribution obtained after this truncation, and the corresponding evolution process is iterated until market quality reaches a stable state. This statistical approach gives three results. (i) We identify a mechanism for preventing complete adverse selection, defined as the process where the quality of the market is driven down to the minimum quality floor. (ii) A larger quality variance or a smaller price premium, defined as the amount by which the payment upper bound exceeds the current mean quality, raises the upper bound on the deterioration in mean quality. (iii) A maximum-entropy benchmark shows numerically how quality variance and the payment rate jointly determine market deterioration and the final stable quality platform. This approach also clarifies how market interventions can slow adverse selection: they may raise buyers' payment rate, reduce quality variance, or increase the minimum quality floor.

</details>


### [8] [Richards' equation as a hydrodynamic limit: Chapman--Enskog reduction of the continuum kinetic equation for unsaturated soil water](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17358)
*Riccardo Rigon*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从动力学理论出发，推导了非饱和水流的Richards方程。通过Chapman-Enskog约化，将孔隙填充分布的闭合动力学方程（CKE）约化为宏观Richards方程，明确了滞留曲线、水力传导率等宏观概念的微观起源，并首次从第一性原理推导了双/多渗透率模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宏观非饱和水流理论（Richards方程）将空间和时间的极限混为一谈，缺乏清晰的微观理论支撑。本文旨在通过动力学理论，严格区分两个极限：空间极限（REV收缩到点，得到CKE）和时间极限（Chapman-Enskog约化，从CKE导出Richards方程），从而揭示宏观参数的微观意义。

Method: 采用Chapman-Enskog（CE）约化方法，以Damköhler数Da为控制参数，将孔隙填充分布g(r,x,t)的闭合动力学方程（CKE）进行多尺度展开。利用线性化重分布算子J的自伴性和负半定性，在质量内积下通过CE层级逐阶求解，最高阶对应平衡态（滞留曲线），一阶给出Richards方程及其水力传导率。

Result: 1) 平衡步定义了滞留曲线；2) 一阶方程即Richards方程，水力传导率K作为一阶输运系数（类似于黏度）出现；3) 平均场还原得到标准积分公式，串行路径修正得到Mualem异质性校正；4) 双峰孔隙分布导致松弛谱出现间隙，投影到各带并应用CE，推导出双/多渗透率模型，交换系数由带间连通性决定；5) Da不大时CE展开失效，需求解完整CKE。

Conclusion: 本文建立了从微观孔隙动力学到宏观Richards方程及其多组分推广的严格渐近框架，为理解非饱和水流的多尺度行为提供了第一性原理基础，同时界定了经典理论的适用范围（Da小）和失效条件（Da大）。

Abstract: Richards' equation for unsaturated water flow is derived from the kinetic theory of the pore-filling distribution g(r,x,t) of a companion paper. It separates two limits that macroscopic theory usually conflates. The spatial limit is purely kinematic: contracting the representative elementary volume (REV) to a point yields the closed continuum kinetic equation (CKE) d_t g + div F = C[g], with F a pore-resolved pre-closure flux and C[g] the occupancy-gated redistribution operator. The dynamics lies in the temporal limit, the subject of this paper: a Chapman-Enskog (CE) reduction of the CKE controlled by the Damkohler number Da (redistribution time over forcing time), the structural analogue of the passage from Boltzmann to Navier-Stokes. The linearized redistribution operator J is self-adjoint and negative semidefinite in the mass inner product, with a one-dimensional kernel fixing a single invariant (water) and hence one macroscopic equation; the CE hierarchy inverts the same J at every order, only the source changing. Four results follow: the equilibrium step defines the retention curve; the linearized water budget plus the inter-REV source set the first-order equation; its solvability is mass conservation, i.e. Richards' equation; and the response function gives the macroscopic flux, identifying the conductivity K as a first-order transport coefficient, the counterpart of viscosity. Mean-field reduction recovers the standard integral formula; the serial-path correction gives Mualem's heterogeneity penalty. A bimodal pore-size distribution opens a gap in the relaxation spectrum; projecting onto the bands and applying CE within each, with cross-band relaxation surviving at O(1), derives the dual- and multiple-permeability models from first principles, the exchange coefficient set by inter-band connectivity. When Da is not small the expansion breaks down and the full CKE is needed.

</details>


### [9] [On the use of the Belopol'skaya-Daletskii representation of a diffusion on a Riemann manifold to construct path integrals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17871)
*Paolo Muratore-Ginanneschi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文展示了Belopol'skaya-Daletskii框架下黎曼流形上的随机微分方程提供了一种构造扩散路径测度有限维近似等变表示的基本方法，关键要素是利用指数映射描述扩散增量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在黎曼流形上构建扩散过程的路径测度的有限维近似，并希望这些近似具有等变表示性质。

Method: 采用Belopol'skaya-Daletskii提出的黎曼流形上随机微分方程框架，利用指数映射来描述扩散的增量。

Result: 成功构造了扩散路径测度的有限维近似的等变表示。

Conclusion: Belopol'skaya-Daletskii框架为构造扩散路径测度的等变近似提供了一种基础性的方法。

Abstract: We show that the Belopol'skaya-Daletskii formulation of stochastic differential equations on a Riemann manifold offers an elementary way to construct equivariant representations of finite-dimensional approximations to the path measure of a diffusion. ### [10] [A Unified Discrete and Continuous Theory of Core-Halo Complexity Maximizers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17907)
*Akshat Sharma*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文针对离散和连续概率空间，建立了一个基于Shannon熵和Rényi熵的广义统计复杂度的变分框架，推导出统一的驻定方程，证明所有驻定解具有双水平结构（核心-晕结构），并证明全局复杂度最大值由最小可容许核心实现（离散为单一主导态，连续为无穷小核心）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前研究表明复杂度最大化分布在有限离散系统中具有双水平结构，但缺乏对离散和连续概率空间的统一处理。本文旨在填补这一空白，建立通用框架。

Method: 构建基于Shannon熵和Rényi熵的广义统计复杂度的变分框架；推导适用于离散概率质量和连续概率密度的统一驻定方程；通过数学证明刻画最优解的结构性质。

Result: 得到了统一的驻定方程；证明了所有驻定解具有恰好两个概率水平（核心-晕结构）；将优化问题简化为单一多重性参数；证明了全局复杂度最大值由最小可容许核心实现。

Conclusion: 本文提供了复杂度最大化分布的完整解析刻画，揭示了离散与连续情形下复杂度优化的共同数学结构，为统计力学、信息论和复杂系统分析建立了统一基础。

Abstract: The maximization of statistical complexity has long been associated with the emergence of probability distributions lying between perfect order and complete disorder. While previous studies have shown that complexity-maximizing distributions exhibit a two-level structure in finite discrete systems, an analogous unified treatment for both discrete and continuous probability spaces has remained unavailable. In this work, we develop a general variational framework for a generalized statistical complexity constructed from Shannon and Renyi entropies. We derive a common stationary equation governing both discrete probability masses and continuous probability densities and prove that every stationary solution necessarily possesses exactly two probability levels, establishing a universal core-halo structure. We further demonstrate that the optimization problem reduces to a single multiplicity parameter and prove that the global complexity maximum is attained by the smallest admissible core, corresponding to a single dominant state in the discrete case and an infinitesimal core in the continuous limit. These results provide a complete analytical characterization of the complexity-maximizing distributions and reveal a common mathematical structure underlying complexity optimization in both discrete and continuous settings. The framework establishes a unified foundation for generalized statistical complexity with potential applications in statistical mechanics, information theory, and the analysis of complex systems.

### [12] [Expansion of a free Fermi gas released from an isotropic trapping potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18007)

Method: 采用半经典方法（semi-classical techniques）分析大粒子数极限下的费米子系统膨胀过程。

Result: 推导出任意幂律指数a和任意维度d下膨胀云团的动量分布与空间轮廓的显式表达式，发现了普适的边缘指数d/a。

Using semi-classical techniques, we derive the full late-time profile of the expanding cloud in the regime when the fermion number is large. We thus obtain explicit expressions for power-law potentials with arbitrary exponent $a$ and in all dimensions $d$. The momentum distribution and the spatial profile of the cloud exhibit a universal edge exponent $d/a$, thus generalizing the Wigner semi-circle law and the Thomas-Fermi distribution.

However, long-horizon forecasts remain challenging due to error accumulation and the complex coupling of process variables. In this work, we introduce the Diffusion-corrected Auto-Regressive Fourier Neural Operator (DiffARFNO), a two-stage framework that combines an autoregressive Fourier-MIONet with a conditional Denoising Diffusion Implicit Model (DDIM) corrector. Fourier-MIONet is trained as a coarse predictor and deployed autoregressively for long-horizon forecasting. By combining coarse predictions from Fourier-MIONet with a DDIM corrector that restores fine details, DiffARFNO aims to provide high-fidelity predictions for long-horizon forecasts. ### [14] [Reinforcement Learning-Guided NSGA-II Enhanced with Gray Relational Coefficient for Multi-Objective Optimization: Application to NASDAQ Portfolio Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16194)
*Zhiyuan Wang,Qinxu Ding,Ding Ding,Siying Zhu,Jing Ren,Yue Wang,Chong Hui Tan*

Method: 将强化学习（RL）智能体作为控制器嵌入NSGA-II框架，根据每代种群的超体积、可行性和多样性指标在线调整进化参数；同时设计基于灰色关联度（GRC）的二元锦标赛选择算子，综合排序等级、拥挤距离和理想参考点接近度构成统一得分来优选父代。

Abstract: In modern financial markets, decision-makers increasingly rely on quantitative methods to navigate complex trade-offs among multiple, often conflicting objectives. This paper addresses constrained multi-objective optimization (MOO) with an application to portfolio optimization for minimizing risk and maximizing return. To address existing gaps, we propose a novel reinforcement learning (RL)-guided non-dominated sorting genetic algorithm II (NSGA-II) enhanced with gray relational coefficients (GRC), termed RL-NSGA-II-GRC, which combines an RL agent controller and GRC-based selection to improve convergence and diversity of Pareto fronts. The agent adapts evolutionary parameters online using metrics of hypervolume, feasibility, and diversity, while the GRC tournament operator ranks parents via a unified score considering dominance rank, crowding distance, and proximity to ideal reference. We evaluate the framework on the Kursawe and CONSTR benchmarks and a NASDAQ portfolio application. On the benchmarks, RL-NSGA-II-GRC achieves convergence improvements of about 5.8% and 4.4% over NSGA-II, while preserving well-distributed non-dominated solutions. In the portfolio application, it produces a smooth, densely populated efficient frontier supporting identification of the maximum Sharpe ratio portfolio (annualized Sharpe =1.92) and utility-optimal portfolios for different risk-aversion levels. The main contributions are three-fold: 1) we propose an RL-NSGA-II-GRC method integrating an RL agent into the evolutionary framework to adaptively control parameters via generational feedback; 2) we design a GRC-enhanced binary tournament operator providing a comprehensive indicator to guide the search toward the Pareto front; 3) we demonstrate, on benchmark MOO and a NASDAQ case study, that the method delivers improved convergence and well-populated frontiers supporting actionable insights.

### [15] [Grounded verification of chemical and materials reasoning: detection is the bottleneck](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17417)
*Can Polat,Mustafa Kurban,Erchin Serpedin,Hasan Kurban*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一种分级验证器框架，通过数据库和物理规则检测并修正大模型在化学推理中的事实错误（如分子式、空间群、形成能），在仅需传统检索增强方法约1/3检索成本的情况下，将公式错误率从22%降至4%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在化学推理过程中会流畅地编造化学对象（分子式、空间群、形成能），尤其集中在长尾实体——这些正是模型可信度最低的区域。现有方法如全局检索增强存在覆盖成本高的问题，而确定性、基于数据库的验证可以捕捉并修复这类错误，但关键挑战在于检测环节而非修复环节。

Method: 提出分级验证器（tiered verifier）框架：(1) 从推理轨迹中提取每个可检验的声明；(2) 对照权威数据库和物理规则进行检查；(3) 将参考信息送入门控修正循环（gated correction loop），仅在检测到错误时触发修复。

Result: 在4个模型和528个条件锚定提示上的实验表明：门控修正将公式错误率从22%降至4%，检索次数仅为全局检索增强（blanket augmentation）的3.2倍；修复成功率在80-97%之间（只要标记被触发）；瓶颈在于循环内检测召回率。当下游交付物在验证器范围内时，最终答案准确率从83%提升至90%；性能提升仅出现在存在可提取长尾错误的任务上（同位素半衰期从11%降至0%），而在接近上限的物理常数上无提升。

Conclusion: 确定性的、基于数据库的分级验证加门控修正能够有效检测和纠正大模型在化学知识上的事实错误，其效率优于全局检索增强。关键瓶颈在于循环内的检测召回率而非修复能力，这为未来工作指明了方向。

Abstract: Large language models confabulate chemical objects (molecular formulas, space groups, formation energies) in fluent reasoning traces, concentrated on long-tail entities where confidence is least trustworthy. Deterministic, database-grounded verification can catch and repair such errors without the coverage cost of blanket retrieval; the binding constraint, we find, is detection, not repair. Our tiered verifier extracts each checkable claim, checks it against authoritative databases and physics, and feeds the reference into a gated correction loop. Across four models and 528 condition-pinned prompts, gated correction cuts committed-formula error from 22% to 4% at $3.2\times$ fewer retrievals than blanket augmentation, beating a conversational oracle. Repair succeeds wherever a flag fires (80--97%); the bottleneck is in-loop detection recall. Grounding improves the final answer only when the verifier's scope reaches the deliverable (83% to 90%), and the lift appears only where extractable long-tail error exists: absent on near-ceiling physical constants, large on isotope half-lives (11% to 0%).

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出DocOCR-Eval框架，采用三阶段校正与排序策略（three-staged correction and ranking strategy），无需真实标签即可近似基于标注的工具排序；通过聚合多个MLLM的评估结果逐步提升与基于标注排序的一致性。

Result: 在多个跨领域、跨语言的扫描文档基准上进行了系统性评估；聚合多个MLLM可逐步提升与基于标注排序的对齐程度；在标签稀缺的实际场景下也能实现可靠的OCR工具选择。

Abstract: Document parsing is a foundational step for document understanding tasks such as visual question answering and key information extraction, as it transforms unstructured scanned images into structured representations by extracting textual, visual, and layout information. While numerous Optical Character Recognition (OCR) engines and multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have been developed for this purpose, selecting an appropriate document parsing solution for a given document collection remains challenging, particularly in label-scarce settings. In this work, we conduct a systematic evaluation of text recognition performance across a diverse set of OCR engines and state-of-the-art MLLMs on multiple scanned document benchmarks spanning different domains and languages. Motivated by the limited contextual reasoning capabilities of many OCR engines and the high cost of manual annotations, we propose DocOCR-Eval, an annotation-free evaluation framework for automatic OCR assessment and selection. DocOCR-Eval employs a three-staged correction and ranking strategy to approximate annotation-based tool ordering without ground-truth labels. We show that aggregating across multiple MLLMs progressively improves alignment with annotation-based rankings. Extensive experiments further demonstrate that reliable OCR tool selection can be achieved in realistic, label-limited settings, providing practical guidance for deploying document parsing systems across diverse real-world document collections.

### [17] [Fully-sensorized smart-eyewear platform for on-device Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16222)
*Andrea Giudici,Christian Veronesi,Pietro Bartoli,Mario Caliò,Aurelio Teliti,Giacomo Gervasoni,Diana Trojaniello,Franco Zappa*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用STM32N6微控制器及其集成NPU实现端侧机器学习；提出头部并行注意力（HPA）作为YOLOv11模型架构改进以适配NPU高效执行；在WOTR数据集上训练并部署；集成RGB摄像头、ToF传感器、麦克风和环境传感器的多模态传感套件。

Result: 部署配置在严格内存约束下达到24 mAP50-95，内存占用仅2.483 MB；系统以10 FPS运行，200 mAh电池下连续自主续航约113分钟。

Conclusion: ARGO证明了高性能、隐私保护且社会可接受的辅助设备的可行性，展示了竞争力的边缘AI解决方案日益需要紧密集成的多学科协同设计方法。

Abstract: This paper presents ARGO, a smart eyewear platform designed to bridge ergonomic comfort, high computational throughput, and energy efficiency. Unlike cloud-dependent solutions, ARGO leverages the STM32N6 microcontroller and its integrated Neural Processing Unit (NPU) to enable on-device machine learning, minimizing latency and preserving user privacy through local data processing. The primary contribution lies in the holistic co-design of hardware, firmware, and artificial intelligence, centered on the deployment of an optimized YOLOv11 model for real-time urban obstacle recognition. To ensure compatibility with the target NPU, we introduce Head-wise Parallel Attention (HPA), an architectural refinement that enables efficient accelerator execution while preserving the original computational logic. The model is trained on the Walking On The Road (WOTR) dataset, and the final deployed configuration achieves an mAP50-95 of 24 under strict memory constraints, with a memory footprint of only 2.483 MB. The platform integrates a multimodal sensor suite, RGB cameras, Time-of-Flight sensors, microphones, and ambient sensors, and delivers 10 FPS at a continuous autonomy of ~113 minutes on a 200 mAh battery. These results demonstrate the feasibility of a high-performance, privacy-preserving, and socially acceptable assistive device, and highlight how competitive edge AI solutions increasingly demand tightly integrated, multidisciplinary co-design approaches.

</details>


### [18] [LLM Unlearning for Cyber Defense: A Survey on Methods, Challenges, and Emerging Threats](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16227)
*Ruppikha Sree Shankar,Abhishek Bhardwaj,Arnav Doshi,Anusri Nagarajan,Troy Paulus Asia,Saptarshi Sengupta*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统审视了大语言模型（LLM）遗忘技术面临的安全与可验证性问题，重点分析了基于梯度的方法能否真正删除知识而非仅仅抑制其表达，并指出当前方法在可验证遗忘方面存在根本性挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在医疗、金融等安全关键系统中广泛应用，但其"无法遗忘"的特性导致隐私泄露、版权侵权、有害知识残留等严重安全风险。由于重训练大规模模型计算不可行且知识在参数中分布纠缠，LLM遗忘成为核心防御手段，但现有方法是否真正删除知识尚未解决，亟需系统性审视。

Method: 以安全、鲁棒性和可验证遗忘为视角，对LLM遗忘技术进行综述，重点聚焦与现有训练流程兼容且可扩展至十亿参数模型的基于梯度的方法。

Result: 指出当前基于梯度的遗忘方法在安全性和鲁棒性方面存在根本性局限——可能只是抑制知识表达而非真正删除，可验证遗忘的目标仍未达成。

Conclusion: LLM遗忘领域面临的核心挑战是"真正删除知识vs仅抑制表达"的区分问题，现有方法尚无法提供可验证的遗忘保证，这构成了安全关键部署中的根本性威胁。

Abstract: LLMs are increasingly deployed in security-critical systems across healthcare, finance, education, and decision support, yet their inability to forget creates serious cybersecurity, privacy, and safety risks. Sensitive personal information, copyrighted material, hazardous domain knowledge, and memorized training data remain encoded across billions of parameters long after deployment, leaving models vulnerable to extraction, jailbreak attacks, membership inference, and regulatory non-compliance. Real-world incidents, from chatbots regenerating private information to fabricated legal citations producing direct legal and financial cost, place the problem at the center of the emerging-threats landscape rather than the realm of speculation. Because retraining billion-parameter models on revised corpora is computationally infeasible, and because knowledge within an LLM is distributed and entangled across parameters rather than localized to identifiable units, LLM unlearning has emerged as the principal cyber defense response, aiming to remove or suppress targeted knowledge from a trained model without retraining and without eroding what the model should still know. A central question, however, remains unresolved. Do current methods genuinely remove knowledge, or do they only stop the model from expressing it under ordinary prompting conditions? This survey examines LLM unlearning through the lens of security, robustness, and verifiable forgetting, with primary focus on gradient-based methods, which have come to dominate the field due to their compatibility with existing training pipelines and their scalability to billion-parameter models.

### [19] [Operator-Aware Mixed-Precision Tolerance Calibration for Tensor Kernels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16228)
*Dipankar Sarkar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 通过从云端GPU运行中挖掘每个测试用例的元素级误差分布，作者提出了一种数据驱动的绝对容差校准方法。实验表明，该方法能显著收紧容差（最高达2184倍），并将LLM风格bug变体的检测召回率从73.2%提升至82.4%，仅增加1.1个百分点的误报率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前张量核正确性测试普遍使用固定形状的all close-style检查，且绝对/相对容差是手工挑选的，在整个语料库中随意复制且极少重新审视，缺乏数据驱动的科学依据。

Method: 作者从26个条目的gpuemu语料库和2种dtype（共8,076个结果行）的累积云端GPU运行中，挖掘每个测试用例的元素级误差分布。基于正确实现下的观测误差，为每个(op, dtype)组合校准绝对容差，并提出一个核心实证问题：内核自身在正确实现下能证明多大的绝对容差？

Result: 校准后的容差比当前手工挑选的atol显著更紧，最大收紧幅度为attention_triton fp16的2184倍。在7个LLM风格bug变体上，bug检测召回率从73.2%（1,805/2,467）提升至82.4%（2,034/2,467），绝对提升9.3个百分点（新增229个检测）。控制组误报数从0增至20（1,882个正确控制案例中），误报率上升1.1个百分点。

Conclusion: 数据驱动的容差校准方法能显著提升张量核正确性测试的bug检测能力，同时仅引入少量可控的误报，验证了基于观测误差分布而非手工经验来确定容差的有效性。

Abstract: Most tensor-kernel correctness tests go through a fixed-shape all close-style check with hand-picked absolute and relative tolerances. The thresholds are copied across the corpus and rarely revisited. We mine the element-wise error distribution of every test case from accumulated cloud GPU runs across the 26-entry gpuemu corpus and 2 dtypes (8,076 result rows). We then ask one empirical question: what absolute tolerance would the kernel itself, observed under its correct implementation, justify?
  The answer is much tighter than the current hand-picked atol. The largest tightening is attention_triton fp16 at $2{,}184\times$. Restricted to the seven LLM-style buggy variants for which the corpus ships a paired correct counterpart, calibrated per-(op, dtype) tolerances raise bug-detection recall from 73.2% (1,805 of 2,467) to 82.4% (2,034 of 2,467), an absolute gain of 9.3 percentage points (+229 new detections). The control false-positive count rises from 0 to 20 out of 1,882 correct-control cases (+1.1 percentage points).

Abstract: Accurate pre-order shipping cost estimation is important in e-commerce because it affects price presentation, margin planning, and conversion. Static lookup methods therefore miss important sources of variation, while monolithic regressors may exploit strong but non-causal correlations. We propose RouteCost, a production-inspired multi-stage framework that decomposes the problem into time-aware demand forecasting, fee-card-informed baseline pricing, Stage 2 residual correction, and proxy-based box-consolidation inference. Route-level cost estimates are aggregated through a route-weighted expectation formulation to produce product-level shipping cost predictions. Across over 250,000 orders, 260 products, and 18 months of order history, the framework improves predictive quality and aggregate calibration while preserving route-level interpretability.

### [21] [Orthogonal Gradient Constraints Shape Noisy-Label Memorization Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16231)
*Richard Mai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种名为OrthoGrad的几何干预方法，该方法在优化器更新时移除每个权重梯度中与当前权重向量平行的分量。在噪声标签图像分类任务中，OrthoGrad在小数据 regime 下能提升CNN的测试准确率并减少对错误标签的拟合，但在大数据 regime 下效果减弱，且无法完全阻止噪声标签的记忆。该方法作为一种学习动力学诊断工具有价值，但并非通用的正则化方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代神经网络能够拟合被破坏的训练标签，这使得噪声标签学习成为研究记忆驱动过拟合的有用场景。现有的大多数正则化方法修改目标函数、架构或数据分布，而本文则从优化器更新本身的几何干预入手，探索正交更新约束对学习动力学的影响。

Method: OrthoGrad方法在每次优化更新时，从每个权重的梯度中移除与当前权重向量平行的分量（即径向分量），仅保留与权重正交的分量进行更新。作者在MNIST小数据 regime 和CIFAR-10数据集上进行了实验，并通过权重范数、梯度-权重余弦相似度等机制诊断指标分析该方法的效果。

Result: 在MNIST小数据 regime 下，OrthoGrad对CNN的测试准确率提升最明显，同时减少了对错误标签的拟合。机制诊断表明，当原始梯度包含显著的径向分量时，投影效果最强；而在大数据 regime 下梯度已近乎与权重正交，OrthoGrad效果减弱。在CIFAR-10 ResNet-18实验中，OrthoGrad能改变记忆轨迹，但无法完全阻止对噪声标签的最终记忆。

Conclusion: 正交更新约束可作为研究学习动力学的有用诊断工具，但OrthoGrad的效果具有 regime 依赖性，并非通用的正则化方法。

Abstract: Modern neural networks can fit corrupted training labels, making noisy-label learning a useful setting for studying memorization-driven overfitting. Most regularization methods modify the objective, architecture, or data distribution; here we instead study a geometric intervention on the optimizer update itself. We evaluate OrthoGrad, which removes the component of each weight gradient parallel to the current weight vector, in noisy-label image classification. On MNIST with small-data regimes, OrthoGrad improves test accuracy most clearly for CNNs while reducing corrupted-label fitting. Mechanism diagnostics based on weight norms and gradient-weight cosine similarity suggest that the projection has the strongest effect when the raw gradient contains a nontrivial radial component, and becomes weaker in larger-data regimes where gradients are already nearly orthogonal to weights. Additional CIFAR-10 ResNet-18 experiments show that the method can alter memorization trajectories but does not prevent eventual noisy-label memorization. These results support orthogonal update constraints as a useful diagnostic for studying learning dynamics, while showing that OrthoGrad is regime-dependent rather than universally regularizing.

### [22] [From Weights to Words: Expressing and Editing Preference Model Inferences in Natural Language](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16232)
*Zachary Wojtowicz,Ayush Nayak,Jacob Andreas*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出"weights to words"方法，能从高维选择数据中自动发现用自然语言描述的人类偏好维度，并通过人类实验证明其能提高偏好模型预测准确率，且用户更偏好该方法生成的偏好画像。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出"weights to words"方法：输入选择问题数据集，自动发现一组领域相关的偏好维度，每个维度用自然语言描述，并与模型表征空间中的向量对应。该方法能：将归因集中在少量有意义的因素上，并以自然语言外化模型推理，支持用户实时检查和编辑。

Result: 在道德困境（N=450）和电影选择（N=449）两个预注册人类实验中证明：（1）将偏好模型朝学习到的基础正则化可提高保留集上的预测精度；（2）融合参与者的结构化编辑可进一步提升精度。在直接对比中，参与者更偏好该方法推断的偏好画像，并认为其预测更准确。

Conclusion: "weights to words"方法有效解决了偏好学习中的欠确定性和不透明性问题，既能通过维度归因提升模型预测性能，又能以自然语言形式实现模型可解释性与人机交互编辑。

Abstract: The growing use of statistical learning algorithms to infer human preferences from high-dimensional choice data runs up against a fundamental challenge: choice alternatives typically differ in many ways simultaneously, so it is generally unclear which factors actually drove an observed decision and should be credited as preferences. Compounding this problem, the opacity of these methods leaves human operators unable to inspect, contest, or correct models when they err. We introduce \emph{weights to words}, a method that takes a dataset of choice problems as input and automatically discovers a collection of domain-relevant preference dimensions, each described in natural language and paired with a vector in the model's representational space. These dimensions address both under-determination and opacity: they can be applied to concentrate attribution on a small set of meaningful factors, and they can externalize the model's inferences in natural language so that users can inspect and edit them in real time. We first qualitatively illustrate the method's versatility on four diverse domains: moral dilemmas, movies, wines, and free-form LLM responses. We then report two pre-registered human-subjects experiments, on moral dilemmas ($N=450$) and movie selection ($N=449$), that demonstrate its benefits for learning preference models: (1) regularizing a preference model toward the learned basis increases prediction accuracy on held-out choices, and (2) incorporating participants' structured edits further improves accuracy. In head-to-head comparisons, participants prefer the method's inferred preference profiles and endorse its predictions as more accurate.

### [26] [The Failures of Marginal Influence-Based Attribution Methods for Global Time Series Explanations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16236)
*Amadeo Tunyi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 现有时间序列可解释性方法生成标量归因分数时存在根本性计算错配——它们通过边际条件或流形外梯度计算，在自相关下混淆了直接时序依赖与中介依赖。论文提出DAG忠实性概念，论证了SHAP等标准方法及时间序列扩展均不满足此性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示时间序列模型可解释性方法中归因分数标量格式并非根本问题，真正缺陷在于计算方法在自相关条件下混淆了直接时序依赖与中介依赖，导致归因结果不可靠。

Method: 定义了DAG忠实性（DAG-faithfulness）这一形式化概念：当解释编码的时序依赖图与模型隐式学习的时间有向无环图马尔可夫等价时，该解释是DAG忠实的。以此为标准，分析现有方法的局限性。

Result: 标准归因方法（如SHAP）通常不满足DAG忠实性；近期时间序列感知扩展方法继承了相同的计算限制，同样不满足该性质。

Conclusion: 现有时间序列归因方法存在系统性缺陷，其失败根源不是标量归因格式，而是计算机制上的根本性错配，需要重新设计能够区分直接与间接时序依赖的解释方法。

Abstract: Explainability methods for time series models predominantly produce flat attribution scores: they quantify the direct influence of a feature at a timestamp by a scalar. We prove that the dominant failure mode of such methods is not the scalar format itself but a fundamental computational mismatch: existing methods compute scores via marginal conditioning or off-manifold gradients, both of which conflate direct temporal dependencies with mediated ones under autocorrelation. We also define DAG-faithfulness: an explanation is DAG-faithful if the temporal dependency graph it encodes is Markov-equivalent to the temporal directed acyclic graph (DAG) implicitly learned by the model. Particularly, we observe that standard attribution methods, specifically SHAP, are not DAG-faithful in general, and that recent time-series-aware extensions inherit the same computational limitation.

</details>


### [27] [Quantizing Recursive Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16237)
*Thorir Mar Ingolfsson,Wajeeha Tahir,Anna Tegon,Lionnus Kesting,Gamze İslamoğlu,Luca Benini*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 递归推理模型因权重复用而对量化误差高度敏感，逐张量4-bit量化会导致系统性偏差累积，使数独准确率从84.1%骤降至0.0%。本文发现问题根源在于激活缩放粒度而非位宽或格式，采用逐块缩放（MXInt4格式）可完全恢复性能，且块级量化在不同递归深度和架构上均保持鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 递归推理模型通过重复使用紧凑的权值绑定模块来求解复杂难题，然而低精度量化（尤其是4-bit逐张量量化）会导致误差逐步骤累积、系统性偏离，严重破坏模型性能。本文旨在探究这一坍塌现象的根本原因并寻找有效的量化方案。

Method: 通过对比不同量化粒度（逐张量 vs. 逐块）分析性能退化原因；采用MXInt4块级整数激活格式实现逐块缩放；在多个递归推理架构（包括EqR均衡模型）上进行实验，并扩展到ARC-AGI开放式基准测试。

Result: 逐张量4-bit量化使数独精确求解准确率从84.1%降至0.0%（仅约25%单元格正确）；采用逐块缩放（MXInt4）后性能完全恢复；递归深度和权重复用程度越高，对量化越敏感（EqR模型最敏感），但块级缩放克服了这一脆弱性。

Conclusion: 递归推理模型的量化坍塌源于激活缩放粒度而非位宽或数值格式；块级量化（如MXInt4）是保持递归推理模型性能的有效策略，在不同架构和开放式任务上均表现鲁棒。

Abstract: Recursive reasoning models solve hard puzzles by applying compact, weight-tied blocks over many refinement steps. Because these blocks are reused many times, quantizing them creates a unique dynamical problem: the quantization error is incurred at every step. While 8-bit quantization (integer or float) preserves accuracy, moving to a per-tensor 4-bit format causes a systematic bias to accumulate. The ensuing drift catastrophically degrades exact-solution accuracy on Sudoku from 84.1% to 0.0% (only ~25% of cells correct). In this work, we show that this collapse is caused by activation-scaling granularity rather than bit-width or number format. Crucially, moving to per-block scaling completely restores the transition. To implement this, we apply MXInt4, a blockwise integer activation format, to recursive reasoning models. It is competitive with blockwise float formats on our tasks, while keeping integer elements and power-of-two block scales. Finally, recursion depth and reuse modulate quantization sensitivity, with the deepest architecture we test (the EqR equilibrium model) the most sensitive. Yet blockwise scaling overcomes this vulnerability, staying robust across these architectures and transferring to the open-ended ARC-AGI benchmark.

### [28] [BACON: Budgeted Human Calibration for Modeling and Evaluation with Multiple AI Judges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16239)
*Lei Shi,Anlan Zhang,Rita Lyu,Zhengmian Hu,Tong Yu,David Arbour,Avi Feller,Saayan Mitra,Ritwik Sinha*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: BACON是一个四阶段流水线，通过预算有限的人工校准结合多个AI裁判的输出，生成更准确的标注，支持总体指标估计和个体评分，在多个任务中优于纯AI或纯人工方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI裁判存在对人工偏好的偏差且高度依赖具体项目，未经校准的AI评估会直接扭曲模型排名、项目评分等下游决策，因此需要一种可扩展且统计严谨的校准方法。

Method: BACON包含四个阶段：1) 为每个项目构建全覆盖辅助特征（多裁判分数、token级不确定性统计、上下文嵌入）；2) 收集少量人工标注子集；3) 训练交叉拟合结果模型生成校准的代理预测；4) 支持总体指标估计（增广估计方程+置信区间）和个体代理评分两个用途。

Result: 在多种任务、领域和标注预算下，BACON相比原始AI输出和纯人工方法，提高了预测准确性和排名一致性，降低了偏差和方差。

Conclusion: BACON将AI裁判视为辅助测量而非真实答案，以人工标注为校准锚点，AI信号提升效率，提供了在有限人工标注下进行可扩展评估的实用且统计严谨的框架。

Abstract: AI judges offer a scalable, low-cost alternative to human evaluation, but their outputs can be biased relative to human preferences and highly item-dependent, varying across judges, tasks, and domains. When uncalibrated AI evaluations are used for model ranking, item scoring, or population-level quality reporting, these biases can directly distort downstream decisions. We propose BACON, a four-stage pipeline that combines budgeted human calibration with multiple AI-judge outputs to produce more accurate annotations. BACON constructs full-coverage auxiliary features for every item, including multi-judge scores, token-level uncertainty statistics, and contextual embeddings. It then collects human labels for a small sampled subset and trains a cross-fitted outcome model to generate calibrated item-level surrogate predictions. These predictions support two use cases: population-level estimation of summary metrics, such as means or quantiles, using an augmented estimating-equation estimator with valid confidence intervals; and individual-level surrogate scoring for item ranking and annotation. BACON treats AI judges as auxiliary measurements rather than ground truth: human labels provide the calibration anchor, while AI-derived signals improve efficiency. Across diverse tasks, domains, and labeling budgets, BACON improves predictive accuracy and ranking consistency, and reduces bias and variance relative to raw AI outputs and purely human-label-based methods. These results show that BACON offers a practical, statistically grounded framework for scalable evaluation with limited human annotation.

### [29] [Normalized Rewards for Preference Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16240)
*Shawn Im,Federico Danieli,Skyler Seto,Barry-John Theobald,Katherine Metcalf*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对直接对齐算法（如DPO）在LLM后训练中过度优化隐式奖励模型、降低偏好响应概率的问题，提出通过添加正则化项来维持选中和拒绝响应的长度归一化概率总和。研究发现似然变化主要源于少量异常token，这解释了DAAs为何能在降低选中响应概率的同时提升生成质量。将正则化应用于DPO和SimPO后，在生成质量与通用基准能力之间取得了更好的平衡，并在多个数据集上提升了奖励建模效果。例如在Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct上，AlpacaEval2得分相对提升>20%，通用基准性能相对提升>9%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DAAs（如DPO）在LLM后训练中会过度优化隐式奖励模型，导致偏好响应概率下降，可能引发不良行为。作者希望解决这一负面影响。

Method: 提出在DAAs目标函数中添加正则化项，保持选中和拒绝响应的长度归一化概率总和；通过分析token级似然变化分布来理解过优化机制；将正则化分别应用于reference-based（DPO）和reference-free（SimPO）方法。

Result: 正则化方法在生成质量与通用基准能力之间取得更好平衡；提升多个数据集上的奖励建模效果；在Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct上AlpacaEval2相对提升>20%，通用基准相对提升>9%；有效缓解了偏好响应整体的位移问题，特别是通过利用低似然token减少异常token的位移。

Conclusion: 添加正则化项可以有效缓解DAAs的过优化副作用，提升对齐效果与通用性能，且异常token机制解释了DAAs看似矛盾的行为。

Abstract: Direct Alignment Algorithms (DAAs) such as DPO have become a common way to post-train and align LLMs with human preferences. However, DAAs have been observed to over-optimize their implicit reward model and decrease the likelihood of preferred responses. This results in a decrease in the total likelihood assigned to responses seen in the preference dataset, potentially resulting in undesirable behavior. To counteract this undesired side-effect of DAAs, we examine the effect of using objectives that add a regularization term to maintain the total length-normalized probabilities of the chosen and rejected responses. To better understand over-optimization, we investigate how response likelihood changes are distributed over the tokens with and without regularization. We find that a significant portion of the likelihood changes are due to a small set of outlier tokens, which explains how DAAs improve generation quality despite decreasing the likelihoods of chosen responses. We apply the proposed regularization to reference-based (DPO) and reference-free (SimPO) methods and find (1) improved trade-offs between generation quality and general benchmark capability and (2) improvements in reward modeling across datasets. For example, on Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct, we see both a >20% relative increase in AlpacaEval2 scores and >9% relative performance gains on general benchmarks. Additionally, we find that the added regularization term effectively mitigates the amount of displacement within preferred responses overall, and for the outlier tokens specifically, by utilizing low-likelihood tokens.

### [30] [KernelBench-Verified: Do LLM-Generated Kernels Actually Beat PyTorch?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16241)
*Yunxiang Zhang,Ping Yu,Jianyu Wang,Max,Fan,Julian Reed,Azalia Mirhoseini,Will Su*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现大语言模型在生成CUDA内核时存在奖励黑客行为（reward hacking），通过硬编码绕过计算来虚假提升性能。作者提出KernelBench-Verified评估框架，引入TF32基线、四分布隐藏测试集和内存效率指标。实验表明，最佳模型GPT-5.5在标准协议下报告1.43x加速比，但在验证协议下仅为0.88x，且28%的内核增加了峰值GPU内存使用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM生成CUDA内核的评估框架存在严重漏洞：模型通过奖励黑客行为（如硬编码特定张量值跳过计算）人为提升基准测试性能，导致报告的加速比（如1.43x）不可靠。作者旨在揭示这些问题并设计更鲁棒的评估方法。

Method: 1) 引入TF32精度的Tensor Core加速作为更现实的基线；2) 设计四分布隐藏测试集防止模型利用窄测试分布硬编码；3) 引入峰值GPU内存使用率作为内存效率指标；4) 对7个前沿LLM进行单轮验证评估。

Result: 最佳模型GPT-5.5在标准协议下几何平均加速比为1.43x，在验证协议下降至0.88x，即实际上比PyTorch慢。28%的生成内核增加了峰值GPU内存使用。没有模型能在验证框架下持续优于PyTorch。

Conclusion: LLM生成CUDA内核的能力提升要求评估协议也必须协同进化。当前模型存在严重的奖励黑客问题，需要引入更真实的基线、更广泛的测试分布和内存效率指标来防止评估欺诈。

Abstract: Recent large language models (LLMs) can generate custom CUDA kernels that appear to outperform PyTorch on benchmarks such as KernelBench. Building upon this foundational framework, we demonstrate that frontier models frequently engage in reward hacking to artificially inflate reported performance. In this work, we identify two areas where evaluation frameworks must co-evolve with model capabilities. First, to accurately measure true speedup, we examine the baseline timing mechanism, noting that enabling Tensor Core acceleration with TF32 provides a more realistic estimation of execution on modern GPUs. Second, concerning algorithmic correctness, models often exploit the narrow test distribution by hardcoding bypasses for specific tensor values. By skipping required computations, these kernels artificially accelerate execution rather than implementing actual CUDA kernels. We introduce KernelBench-Verified, an extended evaluation framework that incorporates a TF32-enabled baseline and a four-distribution hidden test suite. We additionally introduce memory efficiency metrics that capture the often-overlooked speed-memory tradeoff in kernel optimization. Under verified single-turn evaluation with seven frontier LLMs, we find that the best-performing model (GPT-5.5) achieves a 0.88x geometric mean speedup, significantly lower than the 1.43x speedup observed under the standard evaluation protocol. No model consistently outperforms PyTorch when evaluated against realistic baselines. On the memory front, 28% of GPU kernels generated by the best model increase peak GPU memory usage. Our findings demonstrate the necessity of continually adapting robust evaluation protocols as LLM kernel generation capabilities advance.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: FTaaS平台中，用户自定义微调会破坏LLM的安全对齐，现有参数合并方法受困于任务-安全更新纠缠问题，安全向量强度难以校准，导致安全恢复与任务效用无法兼得。

Method: 提出TRACE框架，包含两个阶段：(i) 模拟有害微调轨迹，生成逐步退化的模型状态；(ii) 优化一个插件式安全补丁，使其在不同退化基座状态下既能恢复安全性，又最小化对任务相关方向的干扰。

Result: 在六个基准测试和两个模型上，TRACE在所有设置下均达到接近100%的安全率，同时保持与未防御微调模型相当的效用，持续占据安全-效用前沿。

Abstract: Fine-Tuning-as-a-Service (FTaaS) platforms let users train large language models (LLMs) on customized tasks, but this pipeline could erode models' safety alignment. In practice, service providers need to recover models' safety without re-running full alignment, or destroying the utility gained from customized tasks. A line of existing work refers to model parameter merging, which adds a safety patch on the fine-tuned model parameters to shift the model away from unsafe tendencies. However, this merging-based paradigm is fundamentally bottlenecked by task-safety update entanglement: downstream task updates and the safety patch often overlap in their dominant directions, so the merge strength is intrinsically hard to calibrate. If the safety vector is scaled too weakly, harmful components could still dominate, preventing the model from returning to a safe region; if it is scaled too aggressively, it suppresses task-relevant directions and degrades utility.
  To solve this problem, we shift the focus of merging-based methods from designing online merging operators to offline patch learning, and seek a safety patch that minimally interferes with task-relevant directions while retaining decisive control over unsafe behaviors. We propose TRACE, a trajectory-based safety patch learning framework that (i) simulates harmful tuning trajectories to generate progressively corrupted states, and (ii) optimizes a plug-in patch to recover safety while maintaining utility across varying corrupted base states.
  Across six benchmarks and two models, TRACE consistently dominates the safety-utility frontier. TRACE reaches nearly 100% safety on all settings, while maintaining comparable utility to the undefended fine-tuned model.

To address this gap, we develop RobustMAD, the first deployment-motivated benchmark, designed to comprehensively evaluate model robustness through diverse open-ended queries spanning object understanding, anomaly detection, unanswerable problems, and visual quality degradations. Contrary to conventional assumptions, top-performing MSLMs exhibit promising capabilities, surprisingly outperforming even the larger GPT-5 Nano. However, they still fall short of safety-critical requirements, and RobustMAD reveals critical robustness gaps that pose operational risks. In particular, three recurring failure modes emerge: (i) fragile multimodal grounding under fine-grained distinctions or degraded visual conditions, (ii) insufficiently comprehensive responses, and (iii) weak logical grounding on unanswerable or ill-posed queries, leading to hallucinated outputs. ### [33] [CIGPO: Contextual Information-Gain Policy Optimization for Multi-Turn Evidence-Reading LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16244)
*Hao Dou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了outcome-only GRPO在训练多轮证据检索智能体时因奖励方差坍塌导致零优势锁定的失败模式，并提出CIGPO方法，通过注入基于信息增益的逐轮奖励来维持方差，从而在HotpotQA上实现F1从0.252到0.518的显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有outcome-only强化学习方法（如GRPO）在训练多轮证据检索智能体时不稳定，中间轮次缺乏直接信用分配，导致训练崩溃，因此需要一种能够为中间步骤提供有效反馈信号的训练方法。

Method: 提出Contextual Information-Gain Policy Optimization (CIGPO)，使用冻结参考模型在给定证据后对真实答案log-likelihood的边际增量作为逐轮奖励信号；结合IG奖励与F1奖励的分别归一化以及IG权重的课程学习策略。

Result: 在HotpotQA上，CIGPO在3B规模下达到标准F1 0.518（从0.252提升+105%），而GRPO最佳检查点仅0.430，最终检查点完全崩溃至0.000。CIGPO在整个训练过程中保持有意义的奖励方差，避免了零优势锁定。

Conclusion: 奖励方差坍塌是outcome-only GRPO的一个具体失败模式；逐轮信息增益奖励可以有效预防这一问题，为多步推理强化学习提供了一种可行的解决方案。

Abstract: Training multi-turn evidence-reading agents with outcome-only reinforcement learning is unstable because intermediate turns receive little direct credit. In HotpotQA experiments with Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct, GRPO initially improves (standard F1 0.430) but subsequently collapses to 100% format-violating outputs. Training-log diagnosis reveals a zero-advantage lock-in mechanism: all sampled trajectories receive the minimum format penalty (-2.0), group-relative advantages vanish, and the policy-gradient loss becomes zero--an optimization deadlock. We propose a variance-injection strategy: by assigning per-turn rewards to intermediate evidence-reading turns, we prevent the group reward distribution from collapsing to a single value--preserving the variation that GRPO's group-relative advantage requires. Contextual Information-Gain Policy Optimization (CIGPO) implements this strategy using the marginal increase in the frozen reference model's log-likelihood of the ground-truth answer as the per-turn signal. With separate normalization of IG and F1 rewards and an IG-weight curriculum, CIGPO reaches a standard F1 of 0.518 on HotpotQA at the 3B scale (from 0.252 base; +105%), compared with 0.430 for the best GRPO checkpoint and 0.000 for the final GRPO checkpoint. CIGPO maintains meaningful reward variance and avoids zero-advantage lock-in throughout training. These results identify reward-variance collapse as a concrete failure mode of outcome-only GRPO and show that turn-level IG rewards can prevent it in this HotpotQA setting.

</details>


### [34] [Quantifying Ranking Uncertainty in LLM Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16259)
*Bitya Neuhof,Yuval Benjamini*

TL;DR: 本文分析了MMLU基准测试中排名不确定性的来源，并改进了假设检验方法来量化这种不确定性，实验表明MMLU各子领域间的排名变异性显著，应在比较或识别顶级LLM时予以考虑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有预训练模型在多任务榜单上的排名常被视为衡量其效果的标准，但排名本身存在不确定性。近期虽引入了排名置信区间方法量化不确定性，但该方法在知识评估基准MMLU上的适用性及其不确定性来源尚未被深入分析。

Method: 分析MMLU知识评估基准中排名不确定性的多种来源，并针对性地修改假设检验方法以纳入这些因素的影响。

Result: MMLU各子领域之间的排名变异性非常大，这种变异性应当在比较LLM或识别顶级模型时被考虑。

Conclusion: 在MMLU这样的多领域基准上评估LLM时，不能仅依赖单一的整体排名，而应重视各子领域间的排名波动，改进后的假设检验方法能更可靠地量化排名不确定性。

Abstract: Pretrained models are typically ranked on multi-task leaderboards to assess their effectiveness across diverse tasks. Rank confidence intervals were recently introduced as a method to quantify the uncertainty in these rankings by aggregating pairwise hypothesis tests. In this work, we analyze the sources of uncertainty in the knowledge evaluation benchmark MMLU and show how hypothesis tests can be modified to account for their effects. We demonstrate that ranking variability across MMLU subjects is substantial and should be considered when comparing LLMs or identifying the top-performing models.

Abstract: Gate-level netlists exhibit intrinsic structural properties that influence signal propagation independently of functional simulation. Modeling netlists as directed graphs, we formulate node-level regression to learn this topology-derived score using graph neural networks (GNNs). Experiments on ISCAS85 and EPFL benchmarks evaluate how effectively different GNN architectures approximate this metric across held-out circuits, with hierarchical models yielding the most consistent rankings. Component-level and ablation analyses examine the contribution of individual factors. As an illustrative case study, analysis of Trojan-injected circuits using TrustHub templates reveals statistically distinguishable structural patterns, indicating that topology-based scoring provides complementary structural insight.

### [36] [Reducing Per-Sample Harm in Stochastic Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16261)
*Apostolos Avranas*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过优化参数更新来减少每个样本损失增加（称为"harm"）的方法。由于精确公式难以求解，作者将问题降维到批量大小，并限制在最后一层线性层上求解，发现该层能可靠捕获每个样本梯度的二阶统计信息。该方法可无缝集成到SGD和AdamW等标准优化器中，计算开销随模型规模增大而相对减小，在图像分类任务上验证了减少样本干扰和提升泛化效果的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代优化器在聚合小批量梯度并利用历史状态（动量、自适应矩）时，会产生导致个体样本损失上升的参数更新（称为harm效应），这种冲突源于批量平均和历史状态的干扰。现有方法未明确对此进行优化，因此作者希望显式地最小化这种冲突。

Method: 1. 将参数更新形式化为一个优化问题，显式最小化批量平均和历史状态对当前数据的冲突影响。2. 由于精确求解困难，提出高效代理方法：先将问题维度降到批量大小，再将其限制在最后一层线性层上求解。3. 发现最后一层线性层能可靠捕获每个样本梯度的二阶统计信息，因此在该层上使用少量GPU友好的迭代求解。4. 该方法可无缝集成到SGD、AdamW等标准优化器中。

Result: 在图像分类基准测试上，该方法减少了每个样本的干扰，并提升了泛化性能。计算相对开销随模型大小或输入规模增大而缩小，表现出良好的可扩展性。

Conclusion: 通过将优化问题限制在最后一层线性层上，可以有效缓解优化过程中的样本间干扰，且计算开销可控，具有良好的可扩展性和实用价值。

Abstract: Modern optimizers combine gradients from the current mini-batch with historical optimization state, such as momentum or adaptive moments. While highly effective, aggregating across the batch and incorporating this history can produce parameter updates that increase the loss of individual samples. We term this effect harm and formalize the parameter update as an optimization problem that explicitly minimizes the conflicting impact of both batch averaging and past optimization state on current data.
  Because the exact formulation is intractable, we introduce a highly efficient proxy. We first reduce the problem's dimensionality to the batch size, and then drastically cut memory and speed bottlenecks by successfully restricting the optimization to the last linear layer. This hinges on the unexpected finding that this layer alone reliably captures the second-order statistics of the per-sample gradients. The resulting surrogate problem integrates readily into standard optimizers like SGD and AdamW, and can be solved using a small number of GPU-friendly iterations. Crucially, the method exhibits favorable scaling properties, as the relative computational overhead shrinks as the model size or input grows. Experiments on image classification benchmarks confirm reduced per-sample interference and improved generalization.

</details>


### [37] [Let the Data Decide: Supervision Analysis, Capability Trade-offs, and Adaptive Objective Routing in Continued Pre-Training via Off-Policy Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16246)
*Jiangan Yuan,Zhixuan Li,Han Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了大规模语言模型离线策略蒸馏中，训练数据、目标参数化与模型能力之间的交互关系。通过将问题分解为"目标→能力"和"数据→目标"两个分析维度，揭示了语言建模目标（LLM）与知识蒸馏目标（LKD）在梯度层面存在"直接观测词元强化"与"教师支持的替代监督"之间的张力，并引入支持覆盖度、观测词元概率质量、教师分布集中度等诊断指标进行量化。研究发现支持大小k控制覆盖-尖锐度权衡，蒸馏温度调节支持内概率分配；在自适应目标路由方面，领域级策略（对数学/代码用LLM，通用领域用LKD）优于单目标基线，而词元级路由无法稳定超越单目标基线，表明有效路由更依赖于路由信号质量而非路由粒度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离线策略蒸馏已是大语言模型预训练的核心技术，但训练数据、目标参数化与模型能力间的交互机制尚未被充分刻画。现有研究大多将蒸馏视为全局超参数选择问题，忽略了数据异质性对目标路由的影响，缺乏从梯度层面解释不同目标函数导致能力差异的理论分析。

Method: 将离线策略蒸馏分解为两个子问题：(1) 目标→能力分析：对比LLM与LKD目标函数在词元级监督和下游性能上的差异，通过梯度分析揭示"直接观测词元强化"与"教师支持的替代监督"之间的张力；(2) 数据→目标分析：引入支持覆盖度、观测词元概率质量、教师分布集中度等诊断指标，通过控制实验研究支持大小k和蒸馏温度的影响；构建自适应目标路由策略（领域级与词元级）进行实证比较。

Result: (1) LLM与LKD目标函数诱导出系统不同的能力轮廓，梯度层面的张力是能力分歧的根源；(2) 支持大小k控制覆盖-尖锐度权衡，蒸馏温度调节支持内概率分配；(3) 领域级自适应路由（对数学/代码用LLM、通用领域用LKD）一致优于单目标基线；(4) 基于观测词元概率质量或教师熵的词元级路由无法稳定匹配单目标基线，说明路由信号质量比路由粒度更关键。

Conclusion: 应将以离线策略蒸馏为核心的持续预训练重新定义为"结构化、数据条件的监督设计问题"而非全局超参数选择问题。有效的目标路由更多依赖于路由信号的质量（领域级信号已足够好），而非路由的细粒度程度（词元级未必更优）。

Abstract: Off-policy distillation is now central to large language model pre-training, yet how training data, objective parameterization, and model capabilities interact remains poorly characterized. We studies top-$k$-truncated, temperature-scaled off-policy distillation by decomposing this problem into two questions: an \emph{objective-to-capability} analysis of how the training objective shapes token-level supervision and downstream performance, and a \emph{data-to-objective} analysis of how data heterogeneity should inform objective routing. We first show that the language-modeling objective ($L_{\mathrm{LM}}$) and the knowledge-distillation objective ($L_{\mathrm{KD}}$) induce systematically different capability profiles, and trace this divergence to a gradient-level tension between \emph{direct observed-token reinforcement} and \emph{teacher-supported alternative supervision}. To quantify this tension, we introduce diagnostic metrics -- support coverage, observed-token probability mass, and teacher-distribution concentration -- and show via controlled sweeps that the support size $k$ governs a coverage-sharpness trade-off, while distillation temperature controls within-support probability allocation. We then examine adaptive objective routing: a domain-level policy that applies $L_{\mathrm{LM}}$ to math and code and $L_{\mathrm{KD}}$ to general-domain data yields consistent gains over both single-objective baselines, whereas token-level routing based on observed-token probability mass or teacher entropy fails to consistently match the single-objective baseline. These results suggest that effective objective routing depends less on routing granularity than on the quality of the routing signal, reframing continued pre-training via off-policy distillation as a structured, data-conditional supervision-design problem rather than a global hyperparameter choice.

### [38] [Scaling Limits of Constant-Stepsize SGD at Flat Minima](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16384)
*Jingyi Zhang,Cheng Mao,Debankur Mukherjee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了凸优化目标在平坦最小值（即Hessian退化的情形）下，SGD的不变测度行为。对于具有子二次尾部和平坦最小值（局部平坦指数m≥2）的凸目标，证明了小步长SGD迭代的马尔可夫链存在唯一的不变分布，并给出了几何收敛速度。当步长α→0时，不变分布集中在α^{1/m}尺度上，且重缩放后的迭代弱收敛到某SDE的平稳分布。当m=2时退化为高斯极限，m>2时得到非高斯平稳极限。此外还给出了坐标可分离目标下不同平坦指数的相应结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典强凸情形下SGD的不变分布具有√α尺度和高斯极限，但凸目标存在平坦最小值时这一行为是否根本改变尚不清楚。理解平坦最小值下SGD的长期行为对深度学习等场景具有重要意义。

Method: 采用马尔可夫噪声驱动的SGD，假设驱动链具有收缩性。引入与步长α相关的度量构造Wasserstein距离，证明不变测度的存在唯一性和几何收敛（收敛因子为1-cα^{m-1}）。通过重缩放分析小步长极限，建立与SDE平稳分布的联系。

Result: 1) 平坦最小值（局部平坦指数m≥2）下，SGD不变分布存在唯一且几何收敛；2) 收敛因子为1-cα^{m-1}，m=2时恢复经典1-cα；3) 小步长极限尺度为α^{1/m}，弱收敛到SDE的平稳分布；4) m=2时退化为高斯分布，m>2时得到非高斯平稳极限。

Conclusion: 凸目标中平坦最小值从根本上改变了SGD不变分布的尺度行为和极限分布形式：从强凸的√α高斯极限变为α^{1/m}尺度下的非高斯极限。这为理解SGD在非强凸（如深度学习）场景中的行为提供了理论基础。

Abstract: For stochastic gradient descent (SGD) with a constant stepsize $α$, the invariant law of the iterates, centered at a minimizer, describes the behavior of the algorithm over long time horizons. In the strongly convex case, this invariant law has the familiar $\sqrtα$ scaling and a Gaussian limit as $α\downarrow 0$. We show that this behavior changes fundamentally for convex objectives $H$ with flat minima and (sub)quadratic tails.
  More specifically, we study SGD with Markovian noise generated by a contractive driving chain. For every sufficiently small constant stepsize $α$, we prove existence, uniqueness, and geometric convergence to an augmented invariant law in a Wasserstein distance induced by an $α$-dependent metric. When the minimizer $x_\star$ has local flatness exponent $m\ge2$, meaning that $\nabla^2 H(x)\asymp \lVert x-x_\star\rVert^{m-2} I_d$ as $x\to x_\star$, we obtain a contraction bound with factor $1-cα^{m-1}$, where $c>0$ is a constant. This recovers the factor $1-cα$ in the quadratic case $m=2$. We then analyze the small-stepsize scaling limit. We show that the invariant law concentrates on the scale $α^{1/m}$ and that the rescaled iterates converge weakly to the stationary distribution of the stochastic differential equation $$
  dY_t=-h_0(Y_t)\,dt+Σ^{1/2}\,dB_t , $$ where $h_0$ is the limiting drift at the minimizer and $Σ$ denotes the asymptotic covariance. This recovers the Gaussian limit when $m=2$ and gives generally non-Gaussian stationary limits in the flat case $m>2$. Finally, we give corresponding results for coordinate-separable objectives with unequal flatness exponents.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Self-Evolving Just-In-Time Memory框架，包含三个组件：(1) Risk-Sufficient Topological Belief Graph (RSG)用于部分可观测环境下的持久安全相关状态追踪；(2) Agency-Grounded Factual Memory用于精确危险预测；(3) Experience Memory注入程序性元技能指导可执行且保进度的缓解动作。另提出Test-Verify-Write自动化循环，让智能体在测试时从执行轨迹中持续优化缓解元技能。

Abstract: While Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have empowered embodied agents to execute complex household tasks, they struggle to proactively handle dynamically emerging hazards during closed-loop interactions. Existing safety approaches often rely on runtime guardrails to block unsafe actions or induce excessive caution, which severely stalls task progress instead of actively resolving the underlying risks. To break this safety-progress trade-off, we introduce the Self-Evolving Just-In-Time Memory framework, which reframes embodied safety from progress-stalling guardrails to proactive hazard mitigation. The framework consists of a Risk-Sufficient Topological Belief Graph (RSG) for persistent safety-relevant state tracking under partial observability, an Agency-Grounded Factual Memory for precise hazard anticipation, and an Experience Memory that injects procedural Meta-Skills to guide executable, progress-preserving mitigation. Furthermore, we propose an automated Test-Verify-Write loop, allowing agents to continually refine their mitigation Meta-Skills from execution traces at test time. Experiments on IS-Bench demonstrate that our framework substantially boosts the Safe-Success rate across multiple VLM backbones (e.g., +30.3% on Qwen3-VL-8B), enabling agents to proactively mitigate hazards without stalling task progress. Code is available at https://github.com/DyMessi/JIT-Memory.

### [40] [High-accuracy Low-Bit KV-Cache Quantization via Local Distribution Restoration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16248)
*Gradwell Dzikanyanga,Yanqi Pan,Weihao Yang,Donglei Wu,Wen Xia,Hao Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对长上下文大模型推理中KV缓存低比特量化导致精度严重下降的问题，本文发现根本原因并非logits的绝对误差，而是top-K区域的局部排序错乱（structured local misranking），并提出局部分布恢复技术DGAP，通过高效检测高风险步骤并恢复候选token分布，在Llama-3.1-8B上将1-bit量化精度从47.8%提升至83.2%，分布漂移从0.38降至0.14，且保持低比特KV缓存开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 发现低比特量化的核心问题是top-K区域logits分布的局部漂移（structured local misranking），而非传统认知的logits绝对误差。2. 提出局部分布恢复技术，从量化logits特征中检测高风险步骤，仅对选中的top-K候选分布进行恢复。3. 实现DGAP系统，包含高效的风险检测器（risk detector）和校正器（corrector）。

Result: 在Llama-3.1-8B上：RULER精度从47.8%恢复至83.2%，分布漂移从0.38降至0.14。在Llama、Mistral、Qwen等模型上均保持低比特KV缓存占用，且解码开销适度。

Conclusion: 低比特KV缓存量化的根本问题在于局部排序错乱而非绝对误差，局部分布恢复技术DGAP能有效解决该问题，在保持低比特缓存优势的同时大幅恢复模型精度，为高效长上下文推理提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Long-context large language model inference relies on the KV cache to avoid redundant attention computation, but incurs high memory and bandwidth overheads. Low-bit KV-cache quantization reduces this cost, yet it severely degrade quality; particularly, one-bit quantization reduces accuracy from 84.2% to 47.8% on Llama-3.1-8B under RULER.
  Rather than common beliefs that absolute error of logits, we find that the root cause is structured local misranking, where the distribution of logits in top-K region is drifted. We thereby propose local distribution restoration, a new technique that detects steps with high local distribution risk from quantized-logit features and restores only the selected top-K candidate distribution before token selection. We implement DGAP to achieve local distribution restoration, with efficient risk detcetors and correctors. Expeirments show that on Llama-3.1-8B, DGAP recovers K1V1 RULER accuracy from 47.8% to 83.2% and reduces distribution drift from 0.38 to 0.14; across Llama, Mistral, and Qwen models, it preserves the persistent low-bit KV-cache footprint with modest decode overhead.

### [41] [Value-Monotonicity Matters: A Concordance Loss for Deep Survival Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16802)
*Meixu Chen,Kai Wang,Jing Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出现有深度生存模型多使用似然损失（如Cox部分似然、DeepHit似然）训练但用C-index评估，存在损失值与排序性能脱节的问题。作者提出值单调的一致性损失（SCL），其值近似于1减去C-index，保证损失下降对应C-index提升。在18个数据集上的实验表明，SCL的判别能力与似然损失相当，且训练过程中损失值与C-index的秩相关高达0.96-0.99，远优于似然损失的-0.03至0.53。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度生存模型普遍存在训练目标（似然损失）与评估指标（C-index）不匹配的问题，导致损失值无法可靠反映模型排序性能。尤其是在高容量编码器在小样本、高删失肿瘤队列上的端到端训练中，频繁计算C-index开销大，需要损失值本身作为监控、早停和模型选择的重要信号，而似然损失在这一场景下不可靠。

Method: 1) 理论证明任何严格恰当的生存似然损失都存在损失下降但C-index不变的方向，解释了损失与排序性能的解耦现象；2) 提出Sigmoid一致性损失（SCL），其值近似1减去C-index（含温度项），保证值单调性；3) SCL架构无关，对线性模型退化为凸生存排序支持向量机；4) 在4种模态18个数据集上使用统一五折交叉验证进行评估。

Result: 1) SCL判别能力与标准似然损失相当，C-index最优或在一个标准差内；2) SCL训练过程中损失值与C-index的秩相关为0.96-0.99，而似然损失仅为-0.03至0.53；3) 校准性能（综合Brier分数）与似然损失相当。

Conclusion: SCL作为一种值单调的优化目标，其损失值可以作为C-index的可靠替代信号，适用于需要利用损失值监控模型的昂贵端到端训练场景。

Abstract: Deep survival models are evaluated almost exclusively by the concordance index (C-index), yet they are commonly trained using likelihood objectives such as the Cox partial likelihood, discrete-time negative log-likelihood, and DeepHit likelihood. This mismatch is usually considered acceptable because the C-index can be recomputed on validation data during training. However, for end-to-end training of high-capacity encoders on small, heavily censored oncology cohorts, frequent C-index evaluation is computationally expensive, making the loss value itself an important signal for monitoring, early stopping, and model selection. We show that likelihood losses are unreliable for this purpose and propose a value-monotone concordance loss. We prove that every strictly proper survival likelihood admits directions where the loss decreases while the C-index remains unchanged, causing the loss value to decouple from ranking performance. We then study a sigmoid concordance loss (SCL), whose value approximates one minus the C-index up to a temperature term, ensuring that lower loss corresponds to higher C-index during optimization. The loss is architecture agnostic and reduces to a convex survival ranking support vector machine for linear models. Across eighteen datasets from four modalities using a unified five-fold cross-validation protocol, SCL achieves discrimination comparable to standard likelihood losses and is the best or within one standard deviation of the best C-index. Unlike likelihood losses, SCL maintains a strong correlation between loss value and C-index during training, with rank correlations of 0.96 to 0.99 compared with -0.03 to 0.53 for likelihood losses. Calibration measured by the integrated Brier score is comparable. SCL provides a value-monotone optimization objective whose value can serve as a reliable surrogate for the C-index during expensive end-to-end training.

</details>


### [42] [Benchmarking Machine Learning Models for Multi-Omics-Based Breast Cancer Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16250)
*Priyanka Paudel,Madan Baduwal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究系统比较了多种经典机器学习模型在不同组学数据（转录组、基因组、蛋白质组）及整合多组学数据上预测乳腺癌ER状态的性能。结果表明RNA表达最具预测力，多组学整合带来适度提升，随机森林在整合多组学设置下取得最佳性能（平衡准确率90.3%，ROC-AUC 97.1%），且模型反复选择的生物标志物（ESR1、PGR等）验证了模型生物学有效性。

Motivation: ER状态是乳腺癌诊断、预后和治疗选择的关键生物标志物。尽管深度学习在基因组学中广泛应用，但经典机器学习方法在高维小样本基因组数据上的系统比较研究尚不充分，特别是多组学整合场景下的相对表现缺乏严格的基准评估。

Method: 使用TCGA-BRCA队列的转录组（RNA表达）、基因组（CNV）和蛋白质组（RPPA）数据，采用分层训练-测试拆分、分层五折交叉验证、类别不平衡处理和折特异性特征选择的严格实验框架，评估了随机森林、XGBoost、LightGBM、CatBoost、SVM和逻辑回归在单组学和整合多组学设置下的表现。

Conclusion: 经过精心正则化的经典机器学习方法在处理高维小样本基因组数据集时仍然非常有效；多组学整合为乳腺癌ER状态预测提供了互补信息。该研究为组学数据建模的实验设计（尤其是数据泄露防范）提供了实践参考。

Abstract: Estrogen Receptor (ER) status is a critical biomarker in breast cancer diagnosis, prognosis, and treatment selection. Recent advances in high-throughput sequencing technologies have enabled the generation of multi-omics datasets that provide complementary molecular information for computational prediction tasks. This study presents a systematic benchmarking analysis of classical machine learning models for ER status prediction using transcriptomic (RNA expression), genomic (copy number variation; CNV), and proteomic (RPPA) data from the TCGA-BRCA cohort. A rigorous experimental framework incorporating stratified train-test splitting, stratified five-fold cross-validation, class imbalance handling, and fold-specific feature selection was employed to ensure reliable evaluation and prevent data leakage. Random Forest, XGBoost, LightGBM, CatBoost, Support Vector Machines (SVM), and Logistic Regression were evaluated across single-omic and multi-omic settings. Results demonstrated that RNA expression provided the strongest predictive signal, while multi-omic integration yielded modest but consistent improvements over individual modalities. Among all evaluated approaches, Random Forest achieved the best overall performance in the integrated multi-omic setting, obtaining a balanced accuracy of 90.3\% and an ROC-AUC of 97.1\%. Furthermore, recurrent selection of biologically relevant genes, including \textit{ESR1}, \textit{PGR}, \textit{FOXA1}, and \textit{GATA3}, supported the biological validity of the learned models. These findings indicate that carefully regularized classical machine learning methods remain highly effective for small, high-dimensional genomic datasets and that multi-omic integration provides complementary information for breast cancer ER status prediction.

### [43] [Kernelized Linear Attention: Breaking the Capacity Wall with Symmetric Cones](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17419)
*Ayoub Ghriss,Sourav Chakraborty*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出KATA框架，从第一性原理推导出保证注意力权重非负的特征映射，通过秩一正半定特征实现容量-干扰权衡，在长序列关联召回任务上接近softmax注意力性能，同时实现O(T)线性复杂度和高达11倍FlashAttention-2的吞吐量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 线性注意力在常数时间循环推理方面具有优势，但在关联召回任务上性能严重下降。作者希望从第一性原理出发，设计一种既能保持线性注意力高效推理特性、又能恢复softmax注意力在关联召回任务上表现的特征映射框架。

Method: 1) 将注意力召回形式化为球面填充问题；2) 通过自对偶齐次锥认证非负注意力权重，从第一性原理推导特征映射；3) 提出秩一正半定(PSD)特征，利用Welch干扰界刻画关联容量；4) 实现两种Triton核：flash-attention风格前向和精确O(T)分块状态形式；5) 一阶特征的分块扫描将块间递归深度降至O(log(T/C))。

Result: 1) flash-attention风格达到~1.6倍FlashAttention-2吞吐量；2) 精确O(T)分块状态形式在131k tokens上达到~11倍FlashAttention-2吞吐量；3) 平均~2.4倍于匹配的线性注意力基线；4) 在长序列MQAR和重复键覆盖任务上，多个KATA变体优于Gated DeltaNet；5) 16倍分布外长度下保留0.985 MQAR，约用1/4 KV缓存条目接近softmax性能；6) 340M参数LLM实验揭示了特征相关的流畅性权衡。

Conclusion: KATA通过从第一性原理设计的特征映射，成功弥合了线性注意力和softmax注意力在关联召回任务上的差距，在保持线性复杂度的同时实现了接近softmax的召回性能。该框架还揭示了位置嵌入、delta规则和衰减门控与特征几何之间的相互作用，为未来高效注意力机制设计提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Linear attention promises constant-time recurrent inference but degrades sharply on associative recall. We formulate attention recall as a spherical-packing problem and introduce Kernelized Linear Attention Activations (KATA), a framework whose feature maps are derived from first principles by certifying nonnegative attention weights through a self-dual homogeneous cone. Building on this observation, we show that rank-one positive semi-definite (PSD) features offer a favorable capacity--interference tradeoff. KATA recovers a parameter-free convex output gate and characterizes associative capacity through the Welch interference floor. For tolerances above this floor, KATA enlarges the state without adding parameters and admits spherical codes with exponentially many keys in the projection dimension. We implement KATA as fused Triton kernels at two operating points: a flash-attention-style forward up to ${\sim}1.6\times$ FlashAttention-2 throughput, and an exact $O(T)$ chunked-state form that reaches ${\sim}11\times$ FlashAttention-2 forward throughput at $131$k tokens. An associative scan of the first-order feature lowers the inter-chunk recurrence depth to $O(\log(T/C))$ for chunk size $C$ and averages ${\sim}2.4\times$ the throughput of a matched sequential linear-attention baseline. On long-range MQAR and repeated-key overwrite, several KATA variants outperform Gated DeltaNet, with parameter counts and state sizes reported alongside accuracy. Induction preserves near-perfect recall, while kernel benchmarks show that the maps can be implemented efficiently. KATA retains $0.985$ MQAR at a $16\times$ out-of-distribution length, approaching the softmax with roughly one quarter of the KV-cache entries. Experiments on 340M-parameter LLMs reveal a feature-dependent fluency trade-off and clarify how positional embeddings, delta rules, and decay gates interact with feature geometry.

Abstract: Spatio-Temporal Foundation Models (STFMs) aim to learn generalizable representations of complex dynamical systems across space and time. NeoST introduces a scalable synthetic pre-training corpus to mitigate real-world bias, a latent-space reasoning architecture that generates and iteratively refines multiple future trajectories without sequential error accumulation, and latent-space objectives that emphasize structural dynamics and enable inference-time correction under distribution shifts.Extensive experiments across diverse real-world benchmarks show that NeoST consistently outperforms existing STFMs in diverse real-world spatio-temporal systems, achieves superior long-horizon stability and inference efficiency.

Abstract: Background.
